create table entertainmentgenre  (
        ShowID         int,
        GenreType      char,
    primary key (ShowID, GenreType),
    foreign key (showID) references entertainment (ShowId)
) ;

create table entertainmentcast  (
        ShowID         int,
        CastName       char,
    primary key (ShowID, CastName),
    foreign key (showID) references entertainment (ShowId)
) ;

create table entertainmentcountry  (
        ShowID         int,
        CountryName    varchar(500),
    primary key (ShowID, CountryName),
    foreign key (showID) references entertainment (ShowId)
) ;

INSERT INTO entertainmentcountry
(ShowID, CountryName)
VALUES



create table directedby (
        ShowID         int,
        DirectorName   varchar(500),
    primary key (ShowID, DirectorName)
) ;
INSERT INTO directedby
(ShowID, DirectorName)
VALUES



create table entertainmenttype (
        Movie       char,
        TVShow      char
) ;
